(xds.annotations.v3.file_status).work_in_progress = true;\n19: \n20: // [#protodoc-title: Network External Processing Service]\n21: \n22: // The Network External Processing filter allows an external service to dynamically\n23: // interact with and modify L4 network traffic passing through Envoy. Unlike the\n24: // HTTP External Processing filter, this service operates at the TCP/UDP level,\n25: // providing access to raw network data.\n26: //\n27: // The filter communicates with an external gRPC service that can:\n28: //\n29: // 1. Inspect network traffic in both directions (client->server and server->client)\n30: // 2. Modify the payload data\n31: // 3. Control connection lifecycle (continue, close gracefully, or reset)\n32: //\n33: // Use cases include:\n34: //\n35: // 1. Custom protocol inspection and modification\n36: // 2. Advanced traffic manipulation\n37: // 3. Security scanning and filtering\n38: // 4. Dynamic connection management\n39: //\n40: // The service uses a bidirectional gRPC stream, maintaining state throughout\n41: // the connection lifetime while allowing asynchronous processing.\n42: \n43: // NetworkExternalProcessor service defines the contract between Envoy and\n44: // external processing servers for L4 network traffic.\n45: service NetworkExternalProcessor {\n46:   // Process establishes a bidirectional stream between Envoy and the external\n47:   // processing server. Envoy sends ProcessingRequests containing network data\n48:   // and the server responds with ProcessingResponses containing processing\n49:   // decisions and potentially modified data.\n50:   //\n51:   // The server should handle processing timeout properly to avoid blocking\n52:   // network traffic for extended periods. Any uncaught exceptions will\n53:   // be treated as errors and will terminate the stream.\n54:   //\n55:   // Implementation note: The server should process requests in the order\n56:   // they are received to maintain proper sequencing of network traffic.\n57:   rpc Process(stream ProcessingRequest) returns (stream ProcessingResponse) {\n58:   }\n59: }\n60: \n61: // The payload data from network layer\n62: message Data {\n63:   // The raw payload data\n64:   bytes data = 1;\n65: \n66:   // Indicates whether this is the last data frame in the current direction.\n67:   // The external processor should still respond to this message even\n68:   // if there is no more data expected in this direction.\n69:   bool end_of_stream = 2;\n70: }\n71: \n72: // ProcessingRequest contains data sent from Envoy to the external processing server.\n73: // Each request contains either read data (from client) or write data (to client)\n74: // along with optional metadata.\n75: message ProcessingRequest {\n76:   // ReadData contains the network data intercepted in the request path (client to server).\n77:   // This is sent to the external processor when data arrives from the downstream client.\n78:   // If this is set, write_data should not be set.\n79:   Data read_data = 1;\n80: \n81:   // WriteData contains the network data intercepted in the response path (server to client).\n82:   // This is sent to the external processor when data arrives from the upstream server.\n83:   // If this is set, read_data should not be set.\n84:   Data write_data = 2;\n85: \n86:   // Optional metadata associated with the request.\n87:   // This can include connection properties, filter configuration, and any other\n88:   // contextual information that might be useful for processing decisions.\n89:   //\n90:   // The metadata is not automatically propagated from request to response.\n91:   // The external processor must include any needed metadata in its response.\n92:   config.core.v3.Metadata metadata = 3;\n93: }\n94: \n95: // ProcessingResponse contains the response from the external processing server to Envoy.\n96: // Each response corresponds to a ProcessingRequest and indicates how the network\n97: // traffic should be handled.\n98: // [#next-free-field: 6]\n99: message ProcessingResponse {\n100:   // DataProcessedStatus indicates whether the data was modified by the external processor.\n101:   enum DataProcessedStatus {\n102:     // The data processed status is unknown.\n103:     UNKNOWN = 0;\n104: \n105:     // The data remains unchanged. Envoy will use the original data.\n106:     // This is useful when the processor only wants to inspect but not modify the traffic.\n107:     UNMODIFIED = 1;\n108: \n109:     // The data has been modified. Envoy will use the modified data provided in the response.\n110:     // This allows the processor to transform the network traffic as needed.\n111:     MODIFIED = 2;\n112:   }\n113: \n114:   // ConnectionStatus determines what happens to the connection after processing.\n115:   enum ConnectionStatus {\n116:     // Continue normal processing of the connection.\n117:     // This is the default behavior and allows traffic to flow normally.\n118:     CONTINUE = 0;\n119: \n120:     // Close the connection with normal TCP FIN.\n121:     // This allows for clean connection termination with a normal close sequence.\n122:     // Any buffered data will be sent before closing.\n123:     CLOSE = 1;\n124: \n125:     // Immediately reset the connection with TCP RST.\n126:     // This forcibly terminates the connection without a clean shutdown,\n127:     // discarding any buffered data. Use this for security-critical situations\n128:     // or when immediate termination is required.\n129:     CLOSE_RST = 2;\n130:   }\n131: \n132:   // The processed ReadData containing potentially modified data for the request path.\n133:   // This should be sent in response to a ProcessingRequest with read_data, and the\n134:   // previous data in ProcessingRequest will be replaced by the new data in Envoy's data plane.\n135:   // If this is set, write_data should not be set.\n136:   Data read_data = 1;\n137: \n138:   // The processed WriteData containing potentially modified data for the response path.\n139:   // This should be sent in response to a ProcessingRequest with write_data, and the\n140:   // previous data in ProcessingRequest will be replaced by the new data in Envoy's data plane.\n141:   // If this is set, read_data should not be set.\n142:   Data write_data = 2;\n143: \n144:   // Indicates whether the data was modified or not.\n145:   // This is mandatory and tells Envoy whether to use the original or modified data.\n146:   DataProcessedStatus data_processing_status = 3;\n147: \n148:   // Optional: Determines the connection behavior after processing.\n149:   // If not specified, CONTINUE is assumed, and the connection proceeds normally.\n150:   // Use CLOSE or CLOSE_RST to terminate the connection based on processing results.\n151:   ConnectionStatus connection_status = 4;\n152: \n153:   // Optional metadata associated with the request.\n154:   // This can include connection properties, filter configuration, and any other\n155:   // contextual information that might be useful for processing decisions.\n156:   //\n157:   // The metadata is not automatically propagated from request to response.\n158:   // The external processor must include It compliments Envoy’s health checking\\n27: // service by designating this Envoy to be a healthchecker for a subset of hosts\\n28: // in the cluster. The status of these health checks will be reported to the\\n29: // management server, where it can be aggregated etc and redistributed back to\\n30: // Envoy through EDS.\\n31: service HealthDiscoveryService {\\n32:   // 1. Envoy starts up and if its can_healthcheck option in the static\\n33:   //    bootstrap config is enabled, sends HealthCheckRequest to the management\\n34:   //    server. It supplies its capabilities (which protocol it can health check\\n35:   //    with, what zone it resides in, etc.).\\n36:   // 2. In response to (1), the management server designates this Envoy as a\\n37:   //    healthchecker to health check a subset of all upstream hosts for a given\\n38:   //    cluster (for example upstream Host 1 and Host 2). It streams\\n39:   //    HealthCheckSpecifier messages with cluster related configuration for all\\n40:   //    clusters this Envoy is designated to health check. Subsequent\\n41:   //    HealthCheckSpecifier message will be sent on changes to:\\n42:   //    a. Endpoints to health checks\\n43:   //    b. Per cluster configuration change\\n44:   // 3. Envoy creates a health probe based on the HealthCheck config and sends\\n45:   //    it to endpoint(ip:port) of Host 1 and 2. Based on the HealthCheck\\n46:   //    configuration Envoy waits upon the arrival of the probe response and\\n47:   //    looks at the content of the response to decide whether the endpoint is\\n48:   //    healthy or not. If a response hasn't been received within the timeout\\n49:   //    interval, the endpoint health status is considered TIMEOUT.\\n50:   // 4. Envoy reports results back in an EndpointHealthResponse message.\\n51:   //    Envoy streams responses as often as the interval configured by the\\n52:   //    management server in HealthCheckSpecifier.\\n53:   // 5. The management Server collects health statuses for all endpoints in the\\n54:   //    cluster (for all clusters) and uses this information to construct\\n55:   //    EndpointDiscoveryResponse messages.\\n56:   // 6. Once Envoy has a list of upstream endpoints to send traffic to, it load\\n57:   //    balances traffic to them without additional health checking. It may\\n58:   //    use inline healthcheck (i.e. consider endpoint UNHEALTHY if connection\\n59:   //    failed to a particular endpoint to account for health status propagation\\n60:   //    delay between HDS and EDS).\\n61:   // By default, can_healthcheck is true. If can_healthcheck is false, Cluster\\n62:   // configuration may not contain HealthCheck message.\\n63:   // TODO(htuch): How is can_healthcheck communicated to CDS to ensure the above\\n64:   // invariant?\\n65:   // TODO(htuch): Add @amb67's diagram.\\n66:   rpc StreamHealthCheck(stream HealthCheckRequestOrEndpointHealthResponse)\\n67:       returns (stream HealthCheckSpecifier) {\\n68:   }\\n69: \\n70:   // TODO(htuch): Unlike the gRPC version, there is no stream-based binding of\\n71:   // request/response. xDS Service Definitions in envoyproxy/data-plane-api\\n\\nThe envoyproxy/data-plane-api repository contains 21 gRPC service definitions across the envoy/service directory. These are collectively known as xDS (x Data Plane Services) and define the control plane API for Envoy proxy configuration:\\n\\n**Discovery Services (Core xDS):**\\n1. **AggregatedDiscoveryService** (envoy/service/discovery/v3/ads.proto) - Aggregates multiple resource types over a single stream with methods StreamAggregatedResources and DeltaAggregatedResources\\n2. **ClusterDiscoveryService (CDS)** (envoy/service/cluster/v3/cds.proto) - Discovers cluster configurations with StreamClusters, DeltaClusters, and FetchClusters methods\\n3. **RouteDiscoveryService (RDS)** (envoy/service/route/v3/rds.proto) - Discovers route configurations with StreamRoutes, DeltaRoutes, and FetchRoutes methods\\n4. **VirtualHostDiscoveryService** (envoy/service/route/v3/rds.proto) - Discovers virtual hosts dynamically with DeltaVirtualHosts method\\n5. **ListenerDiscoveryService (LDS)** (envoy/service/listener/v3/lds.proto) - Discovers listener configurations with DeltaListeners, StreamListeners, and FetchListeners methods\\n6. **EndpointDiscoveryService (EDS)** (envoy/service/endpoint/v3/eds.proto) - Discovers endpoint/cluster load assignments with StreamEndpoints, DeltaEndpoints, and FetchEndpoints methods\\n7. **SecretDiscoveryService (SDS)** (envoy/service/secret/v3/sds.proto) - Discovers TLS secrets with DeltaSecrets, StreamSecrets, and FetchSecrets methods\\n8. **RuntimeDiscoveryService (RTDS)** (envoy/service/runtime/v3/rtds.proto) - Discovers runtime configuration with StreamRuntime, DeltaRuntime, and FetchRuntime methods\\n\\n**Service Mesh & Operational Services:**\\n9. **ClientStatusDiscoveryService (CSDS)** (envoy/service/status/v3/csds.proto) - Provides client configuration status visibility with StreamClientStatus and FetchClientStatus methods\\n10. **HealthDiscoveryService (HDS)** (envoy/service/health/v3/hds.proto) - Configures Envoy as a health checker with StreamHealthCheck and FetchHealthCheck methods\\n11. **LoadReportingService (LRS)** (envoy/service/load_stats/v3/lrs.proto) - Reports load statistics with StreamLoadStats method\\n12. **ExtensionConfigDiscoveryService (ECDS)** (envoy/service/extension/v3/config_discovery.proto) - Discovers extension filter configurations with StreamExtensionConfigs, DeltaExtensionConfigs, and FetchExtensionConfigs methods\\n\\n**Filter & Authorization Services:**\\n13. **Authorization** (envoy/service/auth/v3/external_auth.proto) - External authorization service with Check method for request authorization\\n14. **RateLimitService** (envoy/service/ratelimit/v3/rls.proto) - Rate limiting decisions with ShouldRateLimit method\\n15. **RateLimitQuotaService** (envoy/service/rate_limit_quota/v3/rlqs.proto) - Advanced quota management with StreamRateLimitQuotas method\\n16. **RedisProxyExternalAuth** (envoy/service/redis_auth/v3/redis_external_auth.proto) - Redis protocol authentication with Authenticate method\\n\\n**Telemetry & Observation Services:**\\n17. **AccessLogService (ALS)** (envoy/service/accesslog/v3/als.proto) - Streams access logs with StreamAccessLogs method\\n18. **MetricsService** (envoy/service/metrics/v3/metrics_service.proto) - Streams metrics data with StreamMetrics method\\n19. **EventReportingService** (envoy/service/event_reporting/v3/event_reporting_service.proto) - Reports health check and outlier detection events with StreamEvents method\\n\\n**External Processing Services:**\\n20. **ExternalProcessor** (envoy/service/ext_proc/v3/external_processor.proto) - HTTP request/response processing with Process method\\n21. **NetworkExternalProcessor** (envoy/service/network_ext_proc/v3/network_external_processor.proto) - L4 network traffic processing with Process method\\n\\n### gRPC Health Checking Service in grpc/grpc\\n\\nThe grpc/grpc repository implements the standard gRPC Health Checking Protocol (grpc.health.v1.Health) defined in the cross-org domain:\\n\\n**Service Definition:**\\n- **Health** (src/proto/grpc/health/v1/health.proto) - These are collectively known as xDS (x Data Plane Services) and define the control plane API for Envoy proxy configuration:\\n\\n**Discovery Services (Core xDS):**\\n1. **AggregatedDiscoveryService** (envoy/service/discovery/v3/ads.proto) - Discovers virtual hosts dynamically with DeltaVirtualHosts method\\n5. **ListenerDiscoveryService (LDS)** (envoy/service/listener/v3/lds.proto) - Discovers listener configurations with DeltaListeners, StreamListeners, and FetchListeners methods\\n6. **EndpointDiscoveryService (EDS)** (envoy/service/endpoint/v3/eds.proto) - Discovers endpoint/cluster load assignments with StreamEndpoints, DeltaEndpoints, and FetchEndpoints methods\\n7. **SecretDiscoveryService (SDS)** (envoy/service/secret/v3/sds.proto) - Discovers TLS secrets with DeltaSecrets, StreamSecrets, and FetchSecrets methods\\n8. **RuntimeDiscoveryService (RTDS)** (envoy/service/runtime/v3/rtds.proto) - Discovers runtime configuration with StreamRuntime, DeltaRuntime, and FetchRuntime methods\\n\\n**Service Mesh & Operational Services:**\\n9. **ClientStatusDiscoveryService (CSDS)** (envoy/service/status/v3/csds.proto) - Provides client configuration status visibility with StreamClientStatus and FetchClientStatus methods\\n10. **HealthDiscoveryService (HDS)** (envoy/service/health/v3/hds.proto) - Configures Envoy as a health checker with StreamHealthCheck and FetchHealthCheck methods\\n11. **LoadReportingService (LRS)** (envoy/service/load_stats/v3/lrs.proto) - Reports load statistics with StreamLoadStats method\\n12. **ExtensionConfigDiscoveryService (ECDS)** (envoy/service/extension/v3/config_discovery.proto) - Discovers extension filter configurations with StreamExtensionConfigs, DeltaExtensionConfigs, and FetchExtensionConfigs methods\\n\\n**Filter & Authorization Services:**\\n13. **Authorization** (envoy/service/auth/v3/external_auth.proto) - External authorization service with Check method for request authorization\\n14. **RateLimitService** (envoy/service/ratelimit/v3/rls.proto) - Rate limiting decisions with ShouldRateLimit method\\n15. **RateLimitQuotaService** (envoy/service/rate_limit_quota/v3/rlqs.proto) - Advanced quota management with StreamRateLimitQuotas method\\n16. **RedisProxyExternalAuth** (envoy/service/redis_auth/v3/redis_external_auth.proto) - Redis protocol authentication with Authenticate method\\n\\n**Telemetry & Observation Services:**\\n17. **AccessLogService (ALS)** (envoy/service/accesslog/v3/als.proto) - Streams access logs with StreamAccessLogs method\\n18. **MetricsService** (envoy/service/metrics/v3/metrics_service.proto) - Streams metrics data with StreamMetrics method\\n19. **EventReportingService** (envoy/service/event_reporting/v3/event_reporting_service.proto) - Reports health check and outlier detection events with StreamEvents method\\n\\n**External Processing Services:**\\n20. **ExternalProcessor** (envoy/service/ext_proc/v3/external_processor.proto) - HTTP request/response processing with Process method\\n21. **NetworkExternalProcessor** (envoy/service/network_ext_proc/v3/network_external_processor.proto) - L4 network traffic processing with Process method\\n\\n### gRPC Health Checking Service in grpc/grpc\\n\\nThe grpc/grpc repository implements the standard gRPC Health Checking Protocol (grpc.health.v1.Health) defined in the cross-org domain:\\n\\n**Service Definition:**\\n- **Health** (src/proto/grpc/health/v1/health.proto) - Standard gRPC health checking protocol with Check and Watch methods\\n  - Check method: Performs synchronous health check for a service\\n  - Watch method: Streams health status changes for a service\\n\\n**Implementation Files:**\\n1. **Python Implementation** (src/python/grpcio_health_checking/grpc_health/v1/health.py) - The grpc.health.v1.Health service is commonly used by xDS control planes to perform health checks on Envoy instances. Both service ecosystems follow the gRPC protocol and are frequently deployed together in service mesh architectures like Kubernetes with control planes (e.g., Istio, Consul) that implement both the xDS APIs for configuration distribution and gRPC health checking for service observability.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
